## 27. Storage Interface (IStorage)

All database operations are abstracted through `IStorage` in `server/storage.ts`.  
Implemented by `DrizzleStorage` in `server/database-storage.ts`.  
Routes always call `storage.method()` — never raw Drizzle queries directly.

```typescript
interface IStorage {
  // ── Auth Users ──────────────────────────────────────────────
  getAuthUser(id: number): Promise<AuthUser | undefined>
  getAuthUserByUsername(username: string): Promise<AuthUser | undefined>

  // ── Users (Profile) ─────────────────────────────────────────
  getUser(username: string): Promise<User | undefined>
  getUserById(id: number): Promise<User | undefined>
  getUserByAuthId(authUserId: number): Promise<User | undefined>
  createUser(data: { username: string; authUserId: number; source?: string }): Promise<User>
  updateUser(username: string, updates: Partial<User>): Promise<User>

  // ── Food Entries ─────────────────────────────────────────────
  getFoodEntries(userId: number, date: string): Promise<FoodEntry[]>
  getFoodEntriesInRange(userId: number, start: string, end: string): Promise<FoodEntry[]>
  createFoodEntry(data: InsertFoodEntry): Promise<FoodEntry>
  updateFoodEntry(id: number, updates: Partial<FoodEntry>): Promise<FoodEntry>
  deleteFoodEntry(id: number): Promise<void>

  // ── Weights ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
  getWeightLog(userId: number, date: string): Promise<WeightLog | undefined>
  getWeightLogs(userId: number): Promise<WeightLog[]>
  getWeightLogsInRange(userId: number, start: string, end: string): Promise<WeightLog[]>
  upsertWeight(data: { userId: number; date: string; weight: number }): Promise<WeightLog>
  updateWeightLog(id: number, updates: Partial<WeightLog>): Promise<WeightLog>

  // ── Supplements ───────────────────────────────────────────────
  getSupplements(userId: number): Promise<Supplement[]>
  getSupplementsByUsername(username: string): Promise<Supplement[]>
  getSupplement(id: number): Promise<Supplement | undefined>
  createSupplement(data: InsertSupplement): Promise<Supplement>
  updateSupplement(id: number, updates: Partial<Supplement>): Promise<Supplement>
  deleteSupplement(id: number): Promise<void>
  getSupplementCatalog(): Promise<SupplementCatalogItem[]>

  // ── Stacks ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
  getStacks(userId: number): Promise<Stack[]>
  getStack(id: number): Promise<Stack | undefined>
  createStack(data: InsertStack): Promise<Stack>
  updateStack(id: number, updates: Partial<Stack>): Promise<Stack>
  deleteStack(id: number): Promise<void>
  getStackSupplements(stackId: number): Promise<StackSupplement[]>
  addSupplementToStack(data: InsertStackSupplement): Promise<StackSupplement>
  removeSupplementFromStack(id: number): Promise<void>
  getStackReminders(stackId: number): Promise<StackReminder[]>
  getUserStackReminders(userId: number): Promise<StackReminder[]>
  createStackReminder(data: InsertStackReminder): Promise<StackReminder>
  updateStackReminder(id: number, updates: Partial<StackReminder>): Promise<StackReminder>
  deleteStackReminder(id: number): Promise<void>
  getScheduledStacks(userId: number): Promise<Array<Stack & { reminders: StackReminder[]; supplements: Supplement[] }>>

  // ── Supplement Intakes ────────────────────────────────────────
  getSupplementIntakes(userId: number, date: string): Promise<SupplementIntake[]>
  getSupplementIntakesInRange(userId: number, start: string, end: string): Promise<SupplementIntake[]>
  createSupplementIntake(data: InsertSupplementIntake): Promise<SupplementIntake>
  updateSupplementIntake(id: number, updates: Partial<SupplementIntake>): Promise<SupplementIntake>
  deleteSupplementIntake(id: number): Promise<void>
  toggleSupplementIntake(userId: number, supplementId: number, date: string, stackId?: number | null): Promise<SupplementIntake | { deleted: true }>

  // ── Supplement Reminders ─────────────────────────────────────
  getSupplementReminders(userId: number): Promise<SupplementReminder[]>
  getTodayReminders(userId: number): Promise<SupplementReminder[]>

  // ── Disclaimers ───────────────────────────────────────────────
  getDisclaimer(userId: number, type: string): Promise<Disclaimer | undefined>
  upsertDisclaimer(data: { userId: number; type: string; accepted: boolean }): Promise<Disclaimer>

  // ── Meal Templates ────────────────────────────────────────────
  getMealTemplates(userId: number): Promise<MealTemplate[]>
  getMealTemplate(id: number): Promise<MealTemplate | undefined>
  createMealTemplate(data: InsertMealTemplate, items: InsertMealTemplateItem[]): Promise<MealTemplate>
  deleteMealTemplate(id: number): Promise<void>
  getMealTemplateItems(templateId: number): Promise<MealTemplateItem[]>

  // ── Custom Foods ─────────────────────────────────────────────
  getCustomFoods(userId: number, query?: string, limit?: number): Promise<CustomFood[]>
  getCustomFood(id: number): Promise<CustomFood | undefined>
  getCustomFoodByBarcode(userId: number, barcode: string): Promise<CustomFood | undefined>
  createCustomFood(data: InsertCustomFood): Promise<CustomFood>
  updateCustomFood(id: number, updates: Partial<CustomFood>): Promise<CustomFood>
  deleteCustomFood(id: number): Promise<void>

  // ── Training ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
  getWorkoutSessions(userId: number, date: string): Promise<WorkoutSession[]>
  getWorkoutSession(id: number): Promise<WorkoutSession | undefined>
  createWorkoutSession(data: InsertWorkoutSession): Promise<WorkoutSession>
  updateWorkoutSession(id: number, updates: Partial<WorkoutSession>): Promise<WorkoutSession>
  deleteWorkoutSession(id: number): Promise<void>
  getWorkoutExercises(sessionId: number): Promise<WorkoutExercise[]>
  createWorkoutExercise(data: InsertWorkoutExercise): Promise<WorkoutExercise>
  updateWorkoutExercise(id: number, updates: Partial<WorkoutExercise>): Promise<WorkoutExercise>
  deleteWorkoutExercise(id: number): Promise<void>
  getWorkoutSets(exerciseId: number): Promise<WorkoutSet[]>
  createWorkoutSet(data: InsertWorkoutSet): Promise<WorkoutSet>
  updateWorkoutSet(id: number, updates: Partial<WorkoutSet>): Promise<WorkoutSet>
  deleteWorkoutSet(id: number): Promise<void>
  getSessionActivities(sessionId: number): Promise<SessionActivity[]>
  getSessionActivity(id: number): Promise<SessionActivity | undefined>
  createSessionActivity(data: InsertSessionActivity): Promise<SessionActivity>
  updateSessionActivity(id: number, updates: Partial<SessionActivity>): Promise<SessionActivity>
  deleteSessionActivity(id: number): Promise<void>
  getExerciseCatalog(query?: string): Promise<ExerciseCatalogItem[]>
  getActivityCatalog(query?: string): Promise<ActivityCatalogItem[]>

  // ── Training Blocks ───────────────────────────────────────────
  getActiveTrainingBlock(userId: number): Promise<TrainingBlock | null>
  createTrainingBlock(data: InsertTrainingBlock, days: InsertTrainingBlockDay[]): Promise<TrainingBlock>
  archiveTrainingBlock(id: number): Promise<void>
  getTrainingBlockDays(blockId: number): Promise<TrainingBlockDay[]>

  // ── Sleep Logs ────────────────────────────────────────────────
  getSleepLog(userId: number, date: string): Promise<SleepLog | undefined>
  upsertSleepLog(data: { userId: number; date: string; hoursSlept: number; sleepQuality?: number | null }): Promise<SleepLog>

  // ── Provisional Check-in ─────────────────────────────────────
  getProvisionalCheckin(userId: number, date: string): Promise<ProvisionalCheckin | undefined>
  upsertProvisionalCheckin(data: InsertProvisionalCheckin): Promise<ProvisionalCheckin>

  // ── Rest Days ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
  getRestDay(userId: number, date: string): Promise<RestDay | undefined>
  setRestDay(userId: number, date: string): Promise<RestDay>
  deleteRestDay(userId: number, date: string): Promise<void>

  // ── Weight Cut Plans ─────────────────────────────────────────
  getWeightCutPlan(userId: number): Promise<WeightCutPlan | undefined>
  createWeightCutPlan(data: InsertWeightCutPlan): Promise<WeightCutPlan>
  updateWeightCutPlan(id: number, updates: Partial<WeightCutPlan>): Promise<WeightCutPlan>
  deleteWeightCutPlan(id: number): Promise<void>

  // ── Feedback ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
  createFeedback(data: InsertFeedback): Promise<Feedback>
  getUserFeedback(userId: number, limit?: number): Promise<Feedback[]>
  createFeedbackAttachments(data: InsertFeedbackAttachment[]): Promise<FeedbackAttachment[]>

  // ── OFF Product Mappings ─────────────────────────────────────
  getOffProductMapping(barcode: string): Promise<OffProductMapping | undefined>
  upsertOffProductMapping(data: InsertOffProductMapping): Promise<OffProductMapping>

  // ── Training Load Override ────────────────────────────────────
  getTrainingLoadOverride(userId: number, date: string): Promise<TrainingLoadOverride | undefined>
  upsertTrainingLoadOverride(data: InsertTrainingLoadOverride): Promise<TrainingLoadOverride>
  getTrainingLoadHistory(userId: number, startDate: string, endDate: string): Promise<TrainingLoadOverride[]>
}
```

## 28. Server Library Functions

### 28.1 `server/lib/amqs.ts`
```typescript
computeDailyAMQS(
  foodMicros: Record<string, number>,
  supplementMicros: Record<string, number>,
  weight: number
): {
  score: number,           // 0–100 Layer-1 score
  tier: AMQSTier,
  layer2Score: number,
  layer2Tier: AMQSTier,
  confidence: "High" | "Medium" | "Low",
  coveragePct: number,
  coverage: Record<string, { pct: number; absolute: number }>,
  gaps: NutrientGap[],
  topFoodSuggestions: FoodSuggestion[],
}

computeWeeklyAMQS(userId: number, endDate: string): Promise<WeeklyAMQSResult>

computeAMQSTrend(userId: number, endDate: string): Promise<{
  currentWeek: { average: number, tier: AMQSTier, dailyScores: {date, score}[] },
  previousWeek: { average: number, dailyScores: {date, score}[] },
  layer1: { currentWeek, previousWeek },
  layer2: { currentWeek, previousWeek },
}>
```

**Tier scoring (actual `getTier()` thresholds):**
- ≥ 95 → Elite (further capped to Optimal if any critical nutrient < 70% of L1 target)
- ≥ 85 → Optimal
- ≥ 70 → Good
- ≥ 50 → Fair
- < 50 → Basic

**Critical nutrients for Elite gate:** Vitamin D, Magnesium, Zinc, Iron, Omega-3, Calcium

**17 tracked micronutrients (MICRO_KEYS):**
`vitamin_c_mg`, `vitamin_d_ug`, `vitamin_b12_ug`, `folate_ug`, `iron_mg`, `calcium_mg`, `magnesium_mg`, `zinc_mg`, `potassium_mg`, `sodium_mg`, `omega3_g`, `selenium_ug`, `vitamin_a_ug`, `vitamin_e_mg`, `vitamin_k_ug`, `vitamin_b6_mg`, `fibre_g`

---

### 28.2 `server/lib/energy.ts`
```typescript
// MET-based cardio calorie estimate
estimateCardioCalories(metValue: number, durationMinutes: number, bodyweightKg: number): number
// Formula: Math.round((MET × 3.5 × kg / 200) × minutes)

// RPE adjustment factor applied to MET-based kcal for select cardio activities
getRpeKcalAdjustmentFactor(rpe: number): number
// rpe 1–4 → 0.70 | rpe 5–6 → 0.85 | rpe 7–8 → 1.00 | rpe 9–10 → 1.15

shouldApplyRpeKcalAdjustment(activityName: string, type: "cardio" | "lifting"): boolean

// Lifting calorie estimate (RPE factor baked in at storage time)
estimateLiftingCalories(opts: {
  durationMinutes: number,
  sessionRpe: number,
  bodyRegion: "upper" | "lower" | "full",  // MET: upper=3.5, lower=4.5, full=5.0
  bodyweightKg: number,
}): { estimatedKcal: number, metUsed: number }
```

---

### 28.3 `server/lib/training-load.ts`
```typescript
calculateTrainingLoad(opts: {
  durationMinutes: number,
  sessionRpe: number,
  bodyRegion: "upper" | "lower" | "full"
}): {
  trainingLoadScore: number,
  classification: "easy" | "moderate" | "hard" | "very_hard"
}

// ACWR
computeACWR(loads: number[]): number
// loads: 28 values newest-last. acute = last 7 sum, chronic = mean of 28.
```

### 28.4 `server/lib/readiness.ts`
```typescript
computeReadiness(opts: {
  sleepHours: number | null,
  sleepQuality: number | null,     // 1–5
  energyAvailability: number,      // kcal remaining
  carbSufficiency: number,         // 0–1 ratio
  amqsScore: number,              // 0–100
}): {
  score: number,                  // 0–100 composite
  label: "Poor" | "Fair" | "Good" | "High" | "Peak",
  components: {
    sleep: { score, weight, contribution },
    energy: { score, weight, contribution },
    carbs:  { score, weight, contribution },
    amqs:   { score, weight, contribution },
  }
}
```

### 28.6 `shared/weight-cut.ts`
```typescript
calculateWeightCutPlan(
  currentWeight: number,            // kg
  targetWeight: number,             // kg
  fightDate: string,                // YYYY-MM-DD
  weighInTiming: "same_day" | "day_before",
  referenceDate?: string,           // YYYY-MM-DD, defaults to today
  manualTempReductionKg?: number | null
): {
  daysUntil: number,
  totalWeightToLose: number,        // kg
  fatLossKg: number,
  tempWaterCutKg: number,
  weeklyFatLossTarget: number,
  dailyDeficit: number,             // kcal
  isFeasible: boolean,
  riskLevel: "low" | "moderate" | "high" | "critical",
  riskMessage: string,
  milestones: Milestone[],
  plan: DayPlan[],
}
```

**Risk thresholds (% bodyweight / week total cut rate):**
- `low` → < 0.5% BW/week
- `moderate` → 0.5–1.0%
- `high` → 1.0–1.5%
- `critical` → > 1.5%
